   (C)   Violations of speed limits as outlined by this section shall be
subject to penalty as outlined by Idaho law. (Ord. 449A, 9-5-2013; amd. Ord.
556-2023, 9-7-2023)
11-1-25: RECKLESS, INATTENTIVE DRIVING:
   (A)   Reckless Driving: Any person who drives any vehicle upon a street or
alley of the city carelessly and heedlessly, or without due caution and
circumspection and at a speed or in a manner so as to endanger or be likely to
endanger any person or property, or who passes when there is a line in his lane
indicating a sight distance restriction, shall be guilty of reckless driving.
   (B)   Inattentive Driving: Any person who drives a vehicle upon any street
or alley of the city, in a careless or inattentive manner, or in disregard of
the safety of persons or property, shall be guilty of inattentive driving.
(1977 Code)
11-1-26: DRIVING UNDER INFLUENCE OF LIQUOR OR DRUGS:
   (A)   It is unlawful and punishable for any person who is under the
influence of intoxicating liquor to drive or be in actual physical control of
any vehicle on any street or alley or other public place within the city.
   (B)   It is unlawful and punishable for any person who is a habitual user
of, or under the influence of any narcotic drug or who is under the influence
of any other drug to a degree which renders him incapable of safely driving a
vehicle on any street or alley or public place within the city. (Ord. 217, 7-
24-1969)
11-1-27: DRIVING, RIDING VEHICLES ON SIDEWALKS:
It shall be unlawful for any person to ride or use a bicycle, motorcycle, motor
scooter or automobile or other vehicle or apparatus upon any of the sidewalks
of the city; and provided further, that any motor vehicle, motorcycle, motor
scooter or bicycle or apparatus that is operated, driven or ridden through the
streets of the city during the nighttime shall be equipped with sufficient
light to give warning of its presence and approach. (Ord. 217, 7-24-1969)
11-1-28: STOP AND YIELD SIGNS:
Except when directed to proceed by a police officer or traffic control signal,
every driver of a vehicle approaching a stop intersection indicated by a stop
sign shall stop before entering the crosswalk on the near side of the
intersection, or in the event there is no crosswalk, shall stop at a clearly
marked stop line, but if none, then at the point nearest the intersecting
roadway where the driver has a view of approaching traffic on the intersecting
roadway before entering the intersection. (Ord. 342, 7-9-1987)
11-1-29: PENALTY:
Any person convicted of a violation of any section of this chapter shall be
subject to penalty as provided in section
1-4-1 of this code; provided, that upon conviction of driving a vehicle while
the driver is under the influence of intoxicating liquor, the court shall
demand the delivery of the driver's license as provided in section 49-561,
Idaho Code; and provided further, that upon conviction of reckless driving or
negligent driving, the court shall demand delivery of the driver's license as
provided in sections 49-562 and 49-562A, Idaho Code. (Ord. 217, 7-24-1969)
11-1-30: STREET DESIGNATIONS:
   (A)   F Avenue East, from Idaho Street to its intersection with 3000 South,
is hereby designated as a collector street.
   (B)   F Avenue East from Idaho Street to its intersection with 3000 South,
8th Avenue West from Idaho Street to Hagerman Street, H Avenue West from Idaho
Street to West Main and East Main, West Main from Idaho Street to Interstate I-
84, East Main in its entirety from Idaho Street to the Wendell City limit
boundary, and North and South Idaho Street is hereby designated as the truck
route.
   (C)   Commercial trucks, vehicles commonly referred to as semitrucks and
tractor trailers with four (4) or more axles or that is capable of having a
gross weight capacity in excess of sixteen thousand (16,000) pounds, or is
registered to transport sixteen thousand (16,000) pounds or more, are
prohibited from using any other streets within the Wendell city limits, except
those streets designated in subsection (B) of this section, or for the purpose
of local pick up and delivery upon otherwise prohibited streets.
   (D)   Any person to be found guilty or who pleads guilty to violating this
section shall be guilty of an infraction and shall pay a fifty three dollar
($53.00) fine. (Ord. 501-2010, 6-24-2010; amd. Ord. 533-2018, 2-1-2018; Ord.
555-2023, 9-7-2023)
CHAPTER 2
PARKING REGULATIONS
SECTION:
11-2-1: Definitions
11-2-2: General Parking Restrictions
11-2-3: Authority To Issue Parking Tickets
11-2-4: Form Of Ticket
11-2-5: Weight Restrictions
11-2-6: Penalties
11-2-7: Responsibility
11-2-1: DEFINITIONS:
When the following words or terms are used in this chapter they shall have the
following meaning:
 
ACTUAL PHYSICAL CONTROL:          Sitting in the drivers position with the
                                  vehicle running.
                                  All signs, signals, markings and devices
                                  placed or erected by the authority of the
OFFICIAL TRAFFIC CONTROL DEVICES: City of Wendell or by any other official
                                  having jurisdiction for the purpose of
                                  regulating warning or guiding traffic.
                                  Any person who shall drive or operate a
OPERATOR:                         vehicle upon any street or alley in the City
                                  of Wendell or who is in actual physical
                                  control of the vehicle.
                                  The standing of a vehicle, whether occupied
                                  or not, other than temporarily for the
PARK OR PARKING:                  purpose of and while actively engaged in
                                  loading or unloading goods, merchandise or
                                  persons.
                                  Every device in, upon, or by which any person
                                  or property is, or may be transported or
VEHICLE:                          drawn upon a street or alleyway, except
                                  devices used exclusively upon stationary
                                  rails or tracks. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
 
11-2-2: GENERAL PARKING RESTRICTIONS:
Any person who parks a vehicle, except when necessary to allow movement of
other vehicular traffic or pursuant to the direction of a peace officer or
traffic control device, in any of the following designated places, shall be
guilty of an infraction, to-wit:
   (A)   On a public sidewalk.
   (B)   Within any portion of a public or private driveway or entrance to a
public street.
   (C)   Within an intersection.
   (D)   Within fifteen feet (15') of a fire hydrant.
   (E)   Within a crosswalk.
   (F)   Within twenty feet (20') of a crosswalk located at any intersection.
   (G)   Within thirty feet (30') of the approach to any flashing beacon, stop
sign or traffic control signal.
   (H)   Within fifty feet (50') of the nearest rail of a railroad crossing.
   (I)   Within twenty feet (20') of the driveway entrance to any fire station
or within seventy-five feet (75') of such entrance when parking on the side of
the street opposite such entrance, when regulatory signs indicate such
prohibition.
   (J)   Upon any street or portion thereof in a manner which blocks or
interferes with the regular flow of vehicular traffic.
   (K)   At any place where official traffic control devises prohibit such
parking. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
11-2-3: AUTHORITY TO ISSUE PARKING TICKETS:
The City of Wendell, Idaho, through its designated police or contract sheriff's
department, has the authority to issue infraction parking tickets to persons
violating the provisions of this chapter. Said tickets shall be administrative
and payable through the Wendell City Clerk's Office. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
11-2-4: FORM OF TICKET:
The designated police or contract sheriff's department, upon observing a
vehicle parked in violation of this chapter, to leave upon such a vehicle a
separate infraction ticket. For each posted time period, or as frequently as
every two (2) hours that such vehicle has been parked in violation of this
chapter. Each infraction notice issued by the designated police or contract
sheriff's department, shall bear the date and hour of the leaving the same at
or upon the vehicle, the make of the vehicle, the vehicle's license number or
VN, the specific section of Wendell City Code violated and the amount of the
penalty (fine), and shall instruct the owner or operator of such vehicle to pay
the penalty at the Wendell City Clerk's Office, on or before a certain date,
not to exceed fifteen (15) days from the date of issuance of the infraction
notice. One (1) copy of each infraction notice shall be filed with the Wendell
City Clerk' Office. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
11-2-5: WEIGHT RESTRICTIONS:
No person shall park any commercial vehicle with four (4) or more axles or that
is capable of having a gross weight capacity in excess of sixteen thousand
(16,000) pounds, or is registered to transport sixteen thousand (16,000) pounds
or more, whether attended or unattended, upon any streets or alleyways in any
residentially zoned area within the city limits of the City of Wendell, Idaho,
except:
   (A)   For the purpose of loading and unloading materials or merchandise or,
   (B)   For any purpose incident to any lawful construction project located
with the immediate vicinity of such parked vehicle.
   (C)   For any purpose incident to a lawful commercial operation located in
any residential or commercial zone within the immediate vicinity of such parked
vehicle.
   (D)   For unloading passengers and or equipment from vehicles rated for
passenger transportation.
   (E)   For less than fifteen (15) minutes on Idaho Street between Avenue D
and 4th Avenue between the hours of five o’clock (5:00) A.M. and eleven o’clock
(11:00) P.M. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
11-2-6: PENALTIES:
   (A)   All parking infractions issued under this chapter shall be a ninety
dollar ($90.00) fee or assessment.
   (B)   In the event an infraction ticket is not paid within fifteen (15)
business days, an additional five dollars ($5.00) shall be added per day to the
penalty.
   (C)   The failure of any owner or operator to make such payment to the City
of Wendell within thirty (30) days shall give rise to a civil cause of action
against the owner or operator for the amount of the penalty plus late fees,
filing fees and attorney fees. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
11-2-7: RESPONSIBILITY:
If any vehicle is found stopped, standing or parked in any manner violating any
part of the provisions of this chapter, and the identity of the operator cannot
be determined, the owner in who's name the vehicle is registered or the named
lessee in a rental or leased vehicle shall be held prima facie responsible for
such violation. (Ord. 504-2019, 9-5-2019)
